 to sochaa ki baat karte hai

 jisamen bharat or indonesia bhi shaamil hai

com

 malaria se hone vaali har maut kii reporting hoti hi ho iskaa koi thos pramaan nahin miltaa he

 ye argent maamla he lekin mahaz ghoshnaa se kuch hasil nahin hoga
 Sixty years ago, Sri Lanka was considered the most affected by malaria in the world
 pichley saadhe teen saal main srilanka main ek bhi malaria kaa mariz nahin hua he
 Sri Lanka started an anti-malarial campaign in 1911, during which 1
5 million cases of malaria were reported every year
 srilanka ne 1963 tak malaria ko kareeb kareeb khatm hi kar diya tha jab sirf 17 cese report hue
 Then Sri Lanka spent its budget elsewhere
 or machhar phir se lautne lage
 Again it took fifty years to become malaria free
 srilanka main bharat se chaar guna zyaada barish hoti he
 According to the World Health Organization (WHO), Sri Lanka changed its strategy to combat malaria in the nineties
 isamen machhar ke alaava malaria ke parasite yani paraseete ko bhi nishaanaa banaaya gaya
 In the common tongue, we understood that we start fogging to ward off mosquitoes
 lekin parasite ko nishaanaa banane kaa matlab he machhar ke bheetar jo malaria ke tatv hai unhen khatm karnaa
 Sri Lanka used the Internet to combat malaria
 har tarah ke bukhaar ke mariz kaa malaria ke liye bhi test kiya gaya or har cese swasthy mantralay ke anti malaria muhim ko notiphoi kiya gaya
 a national data of this was prepared
 malaria grasit mulkon main yatra karne waalon kii pahchaan kii gai
 They were monitored
 shanti mishan par duusare mulkon par gaye sena ke logon kaa bhi test kiya gaya
 Malaria medicines were only available with the anti-malarial campaign, due to which the private health center was also forced to tell that they had malaria patients here
 anti malaria campan ne 24 ghante kii ek hotline chalaai
 Treat patients separately to prevent the spread of the disease
 srilanka cabinet kaa faisla he ki malaria mukti abhiyaan ko har saal das fisadi adhik bajet milegaa or miltaa he
 In this whole case, two words will be mentioned
 vector or parasite
 Vector means the carrier
 jo dhota he
 Vector means mosquito
 femail anophyles machhar
 The parasite Plasmodium is inside this mosquito and when the mosquito bites, the parasite enters the human and gives rise to malaria-like disease
 srilanka ke abhiyaan ne is palasmodium parasite kaa ilaaj karne kaa sochaa

 On this day, a Somnath temple was attacked and demolished in 12 Jyotirlingas of India
 saal 1026 main mahmud gaznavi ne somnath mandir ko nasht kar diya tha
 It is said that after seeing the mention of the temple in his travelogue of the Arab traveler al-beruni, Ghaznavi attacked this temple with about 5000 companions
 is hamale main gaznavi ne mandir kii sampatti luti or hamale main hajaaron log bhi maare gaye the
 After this it was rebuilt by Raja Bhima of Gujarat and King Bhoj of Malwa
 haalanki gaznavi se pehle bhi somnath mandir par kai hamale ho chuke the or uske baad bhi mandir par hamale kiye gaye
 This temple was broken and rebuilt many times due to its immense luxury
 gaznavi ke 17 hamale jhelkar bhi khadaa he somnath mandirkai baar hue the somnath mandir par hamalekaha jaataa he ki sabase pehle ek mandir isa ke purv main astitv main tha jis jagah par duusari baar mandir kaa punarnirmaan saatvin sadi main vallabhi ke maitra raajaaon ne kiya
 In the eighth century, the Arab governor of Sindh, Junaid, sent his army to destroy it
 pratihaar raja nagabhatta ne 815 isvi main iskaa teesri baar punarnirmaan kiya
 The temple continued to be repeatedly refuted and renovated
 gaznavi ke hamale ke baad gujarat ke raja bhim or malwa ke raja bhoj ne iskaa rnirmaan karaayaa
 When the Delhi Sultanate occupied Gujarat in the year 1297, it was again demolished
 mughal badshaah aurangzeb ne ise punah 1706 main gira diya
 Explain that the temple that stands at this time was built by Sardar Vallabhbhai Patel, the former Home Minister of India

 Sluggish lifestyle, stale eating habits and obesity in Indian girls are increasing the chances of spreading polycystic ovary syndrome (PCOS)
 swasthya visheshgyon ne bataaya ki ek anumaan ke mutabik, 10 se 30 fisadi mahilaayein isse prabhavit ho rahi hai
 Ranjana Sharma, senior obstetrician consultant at Indraprastha Hospital, said, 'obesity and PCOS are closely related, especially when it occurs during adolescence
 pisioes kii ghatana bad rahi he or jeevanstyli main parivartan ho rahaa he, poshan or aahaar isamen bahut ahm bhoomika adaa karte hai
 Agreeing Ranjana Sharma, Sandeep Chaddha, Executive Advisor, Gynecology Department at JP Hospital Noida, said that hormonal imbalances are 'guilty' in PCOS cases
 unhone kaha, 'pichley ek dashak mentanbehaal jeevanstyli hormonal badlaav ke liye pehla kaaran ban chuki he, or isse pisioes kii sambhaavna bad jaati he
 If we look at urban India, every year around 15% of the girls fall prey to PCOS
 'pisioes se andashay main kai tarah ke ulcer banate hai or androgen (purush hormone) kaa zyada utpaadan hone lagata he
 This causes hair on the body and face, irregularities in periods and pimples

 'however, not everyone who has PCOS has all these symptoms
